				add_idea = liberal_democracy
			}
		}
		else={
			add_ideas = liberal_democracy
		}
		
		if={
			limit = { has_idea = wartime_censorship }
			swap_ideas={
				remove_idea = wartime_censorship
				add_idea = free_press
			}
		}
		else={
			add_ideas = free_press
		}
		
		if={
			limit = { valerii_zaluzhnyi_is_leader = yes }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neoliberal
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
